# 🇩🇪 Work in Germany — Automated Job Board

![Jobs](https://img.shields.io/badge/jobs-3537-blue)
![Visa Friendly](https://img.shields.io/badge/visa%20friendly-1019-green)
![English OK](https://img.shields.io/badge/english%20OK-88-orange)
![Companies](https://img.shields.io/badge/companies-1437-purple)
![Updated](https://img.shields.io/badge/updated-every%206%20hours-success)

> **Fully automated** list of tech jobs in Germany, scraped from **1437 company career pages** and updated every 6 hours.

> 🔄 Unlike manual lists, this repo uses **100+ company APIs** (Greenhouse, Lever) and updates automatically via GitHub Actions.
> Every listing is tagged with language requirements and visa sponsorship status.

> 🙏 **Contribute** by submitting an [issue](../../issues/new/choose)! See [contribution guidelines](CONTRIBUTING.md).
